# Creation of the Jarldom of Lindsey
narrative_event = {
	id = 314101
	title = "EVTNAME314101"
	desc = "EVTDESC314101"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_gate"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = d_lindsey
		NOT = { has_global_flag = lindsey_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created }
			}
			c_lindum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
			c_caistor = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
			c_ad_abum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
			c_banovallum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
			c_luda = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
		}		
		d_lindsey = { de_jure_liege = k_northumbria }
		
		d_lindum = { destroy_landed_title = d_lindum }
		
		set_global_flag = lindsey_created
		
		if = {						# Creation by Bretwalda of Aenglaland
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_aengland
					ai = yes
					any_vassal = { has_landed_title = k_northumbria }
				}
			}
			k_northumbria = {
				holder_scope = {
					d_lindsey = {
						grant_title = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314101"
	}
}

# Creation of the Jarldom of Pegansaete
narrative_event = {
	id = 314102
	title = "EVTNAME314102"
	desc = "EVTDESC314102"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_traveller_hills"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = d_mercia
		NOT = { has_global_flag = pegansaete_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created }
			}
			c_trent_hills = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
			c_aquae_arnemetiae = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
			c_segelocum = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
			c_scarsdale = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
		}
		
		c_dovedale = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
		
		d_mercia = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		
		d_the_peak = { destroy_landed_title = d_the_peak }
		set_global_flag = pegansaete_created
		
		if = {						# Creation by Bretwalda of Aenglaland
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_aengland
					ai = yes
					any_vassal = { has_landed_title = k_mercia }
				}
			}
			k_mercia = {
				holder_scope = {
					d_mercia = {
						grant_title = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314102"
	}
}
# Creation of the Jarldom of Middle Anglia
narrative_event = {
	id = 3141020
	title = "EVTNAME3141020"
	desc = "EVTDESC3141020"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_fields_landscape"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = d_middle_angles
		NOT = { has_global_flag = middleangles_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created }
			}
			c_ratae = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
			c_ad_pontem = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
			c_margidunum = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
			c_vernemetum = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
			c_causennae = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = southernboroughs_created }
			}
			c_gwash = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
			c_bannaventa = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
			c_ciniubantum = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
		}
		
		c_brinavae = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
		c_lactodorum = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = aelle_ruling_anglia
				NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_collapsed }
			}
			d_middle_angles = { de_jure_liege = k_anglia }
		}
		else = {
			d_middle_angles = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		}
		
		set_global_flag = middleangles_created
		
		if = {						# Creation by Bretwalda of Aenglaland
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_aengland
					ai = yes
					any_vassal = { has_landed_title = k_mercia }
				}
			}
			k_mercia = {
				holder_scope = {
					d_middle_angles = {
						grant_title = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3141020"
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC3141040"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_hills_woodland"
	
	only_playable = yes

		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = d_cilternsaete
		NOT = { has_global_flag = cilternsaete_created }		
	}

		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c_alchester = { de_jure_liege = d_cilternsaete }
		c_chiltern_hills = { de_jure_liege = d_cilternsaete }
		c_magiovinium = { de_jure_liege = d_cilternsaete }
		c_durocobrivis = { de_jure_liege = d_cilternsaete }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = southernboroughs_created }
			}
			c_durocobrivis = { de_jure_liege = d_cilternsaete }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = aelle_ruling_anglia 
				NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_collapsed }
			}
			d_cilternsaete = { de_jure_liege = k_anglia }
		}
		else = {

				ROOT = {

					any_vassal = { has_landed_title = k_mercia }
				}
			}
			k_mercia = {
				holder_scope = {
					d_cilternsaete = {
						grant_title = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3141040"
	}

# Creation of the Kingdom of Mercia
narrative_event = {
	id = 314105
	title = "EVTNAME314105"
	desc = "EVTDESC314105"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_hill"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = k_mercia
		NOT = { has_global_flag = mercia_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		d_mercia = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		d_magonsaete = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		d_hwicce = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_landed_title = c_letocetum
							any_vassal = {
								has_landed_title = c_letocetum
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = { add_claim = c_letocetum }
		}
		#k_mercia = {
		#	holder_scope = {
		#		capital_scope = {
		#			culture = ROOT
		#		}
		#	}
		#}
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			employer = k_mercia
			female = no
			age = 42
			attributes = {
				martial = 9
				diplomacy = 11
				stewardship = 13
			}
			trait = fortune_builder
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = loyal
			trait = greedy
			trait = diligent
		}
		set_global_flag = mercia_created
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314105"
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = 314232
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	hide_new = yes
	
	ai = yes
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		year = 570
		OR = {
			year = 590
			has_landed_title = d_iclingas
			has_character_flag = mercia_invader
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = mercia_created }
				has_claim = k_mercia
			}
		}
		age = 20
		ai = yes
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		prisoner = no
		num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 4
		prestige = 400
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_mercia
			has_landed_title = d_tomsaete
			has_landed_title = d_wrocensaete
			has_landed_title = d_middle_angles
			has_landed_title = d_magonsaete
			AND = {
				has_landed_title = d_hwicce
				year = 600
			}
		}
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		NOT = { trait = imbecile }
		NOT = { trait = blinded }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_cantia }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_sussex }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_mercia }
		k_mercia = { has_holder = no }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = mercia_assigned }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = mercia_assigned
		k_mercia = { gain_title = ROOT }
		wealth = 100
		character_event = { id = 31205 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}
# Spears of Mercia
character_event = {
	id = 3141051
	desc = "EVTDESC3141051"
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army_banners"
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = k_mercia
		location = { is_capital = yes }
		NOT = { realm_size = 40 }
		NOT = { num_of_king_titles = 2 }
		NOT = { is_title_active = d_spears_of_mercia }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	
	immediate = {
		activate_title = { title = d_spears_of_mercia status = yes }
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			employer = k_mercia
			female = no
			age = 35
			attributes = {
				martial = 12
				diplomacy = 12
				stewardship = 10
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = loyal
			trait = rough_terrain_leader
			trait = lustful
		}
		new_character = {
			d_spears_of_mercia = { 
				gain_title = PREV
			}
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		}
		d_spears_of_mercia = { 
			holder_scope = {
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3141051"
		k_mercia = { holder_scope = { prestige = 50 } }
	}
}

# Creation of the Jarldom of Hampshire
narrative_event = {
	id = 314108
	title = "EVTNAME314108"
	desc = "EVTDESC314108"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_valley_rock"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = d_hampshire
		NOT = { has_global_flag = hampshire_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c_clausentum = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
		c_vectis = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_conquered }
					has_global_flag = meonware_destroyed
				}
			}
			c_venta = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
			c_portus_adurni = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
			c_vindomis = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
			c_calleva = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
		}
		
		d_hampshire = { de_jure_liege = k_wessex }
		
		set_global_flag = hampshire_created
		
		if = {						# Creation by Bretwalda of Aenglaland
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_aengland
					ai = yes
					any_vassal = { has_landed_title = k_wessex }
				}
			}
			k_wessex = {
				holder_scope = {
					d_hampshire = {
						grant_title = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = meonware_conquered
				NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_destroyed }
				ai = yes
				has_landed_title = d_west_saxons
			}
			add_claim = c_venta
			add_claim = c_portus_adurni
			add_claim = c_vindomis
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314108"
	}
}

# Creation/Conquest of the Jarldom of Meonware
narrative_event = {
	id = 3141080
	title = "EVTNAME3141080"
	desc = EVTDESC3141080
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
		
	picture = "GFX_evt_valley_rock"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		completely_controls = c_venta
		completely_controls = c_portus_adurni
		completely_controls = c_vindomis
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_wessex }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = hampshire_created }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_conquered }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_destroyed }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		d_the_belgae = { de_jure_liege = k_sussex }
		d_the_belgae = {
			set_name = "Meonware"
			adjective = "Meonwara"
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = berkshire_created
			}
			c_calleva = { de_jure_liege = d_berkshire }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				d_the_belgae = { 
					has_holder = yes
					holder_scope = {
						NOT = { culture_group = germanic }
						tier = DUKE
						num_of_duke_titles = 1
					}
				}
			}
			d_the_belgae = { 
				holder_scope = {
					liege = {
						PREV = {
							any_vassal = {
								limit = { tier = COUNT }
								set_defacto_liege = PREVPREV
							}
						}
						PREVPREV = { usurp_title_only = ROOT }
						set_defacto_vassal = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = meonware_conquered			
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3141080"
	}
}
# Destruction of Meonware
narrative_event = {
	id = 3141082
	title = "EVTNAME3141082"
	desc = EVTDESC3141082
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
		
	picture = "GFX_evt_valley_rock"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		completely_controls = c_venta
		completely_controls = c_portus_adurni
		completely_controls = c_vindomis
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = k_wessex
			has_landed_title = d_hampshire
			has_landed_title = d_west_saxons
		}
		NOR = {
			AND = {
				has_landed_title = d_the_belgae
				NOR = { 
					has_landed_title = d_hampshire 
					has_landed_title = k_wessex
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				has_landed_title = d_the_belgae
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = hampshire_created
		has_global_flag = meonware_conquered
		NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_destroyed }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		d_the_belgae = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = belgae_created }
				de_jure_liege = k_belgae
			}
			else = {			
				de_jure_liege = k_dumnonia
			}
			set_name = "The Belgae"
			adjective = "Belgic"
			destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
		c_venta = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
		c_portus_adurni = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
		c_vindomis = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
		c_calleva = { de_jure_liege = d_hampshire }
		set_global_flag = meonware_destroyed			
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3141082"
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 314231
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	hide_new = yes
	
	ai = yes
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		year = 535
		#age = 20
		is_adult = yes
		ai = yes
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		prisoner = no
		num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 4
		prestige = 400
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_somerset
			has_landed_title = d_dorset
			has_landed_title = d_hampshire
			has_landed_title = d_devon
			has_landed_title = d_berkshire
		}
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		NOT = { trait = imbecile }
		NOT = { trait = blinded }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_cantia }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_sussex }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_wessex }
		k_wessex = { has_holder = no }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = wessex_assigned }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = wessex_assigned
		k_wessex = { gain_title = ROOT }
		wealth = 100
		character_event = { id = 31205 }
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = no
			age = 35
			attributes = {
				martial = 11
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
		}
		location = { 
			new_character = {
				spawn_unit = {
					province = PREV
					troops =
					{
						heavy_infantry = { 600 600 }
						pikemen = { 300 300 }
					}
					attrition = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

	id = 3141251
	desc = "EVTDESC3141251"
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army_banners"
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = k_wessex
		location = { is_capital = yes }
		NOT = { realm_size = 40 }
		NOT = { num_of_king_titles = 2 }
		OR = {
			NOT = { is_title_active = d_swords_of_wessex }
			d_swords_of_wessex = {
				has_holder = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	
	immediate = {
		activate_title = { title = d_swords_of_wessex status = yes }
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			employer = k_wessex
			female = no
			age = 29
			attributes = {
				martial = 11
				diplomacy = 8
				stewardship = 10
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = loyal
			trait = flat_terrain_leader
			trait = cruel
		}
		new_character = {
			d_swords_of_wessex = { 
				gain_title = PREV
			}
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		}
		d_swords_of_wessex = { 
			holder_scope = {
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3141251"
		k_wessex = { holder_scope = { prestige = 50 } }
	}

	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = k_sussex
		location = { is_capital = yes }
		NOT = { realm_size = 40 }
		NOT = { num_of_king_titles = 2 }
		NOT = { is_title_active = d_swords_of_sussex }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	
	immediate = {
		activate_title = { title = d_swords_of_sussex status = yes }
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			employer = k_sussex
			female = no
			age = 32
			attributes = {
				martial = 10
				diplomacy = 8
				stewardship = 5
			}
			trait = skilled_tactician
			trait = veteran
			trait = patient
			trait = loyal
			trait = rough_terrain_leader
			trait = wroth
		}
		new_character = {
			d_swords_of_sussex = { 
				gain_title = PREV
			}
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		}
		d_swords_of_sussex = { 
			holder_scope = {
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3142342"
		k_sussex = { holder_scope = { prestige = 50 } }
	}
}

# Creation of the Kingdom of East Seaxe (with de jure changes)
narrative_event = {
	id = 314235
	title = "EVTNAME314235"
	desc = "EVTDESC314235"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_lord_overlooking_bridge"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = k_eastseaxe
		NOR = { 
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
			has_global_flag = essex_created
			d_eastseaxe = { de_jure_liege = k_eastseaxe }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		d_eastseaxe = { de_jure_liege = k_eastseaxe }
		d_middleseaxe = { de_jure_liege = k_eastseaxe }
		d_grentbryce = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		d_middle_angles = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		d_cilternsaete = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		d_norfolc = { de_jure_liege = k_east_anglia }
		d_southfolc = { de_jure_liege = k_east_anglia }

		k_east_anglia = { 
			activate_title = { title = THIS status = yes }
			k_anglia = {
				if = { 
					limit = { has_holder = yes }
					holder_scope = {
						grant_title = k_east_anglia 
					}
				}
			}
			#insert_title_history = k_anglia
		}
		
		k_anglia = { 
			destroy_landed_title = THIS
			activate_title = { title = THIS status = no }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					NOR = {
						has_landed_title = c_londinium
						any_vassal = {
							has_landed_title = c_londinium
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = { add_claim = c_londinium }
		}
		
		set_global_flag = anglia_collapsed
		set_global_flag = essex_created
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314235"
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3142350
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	hide_new = yes
	
	ai = yes
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		year = 525
		age = 20
		ai = yes
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		prisoner = no
		lower_tier_than = king
		prestige = 200
		num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 3
		primary_title = {
			OR = {
				title = d_eastseaxe 
				title = d_middleseaxe
			}
		}
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		NOT = { trait = imbecile }
		NOT = { trait = blinded }
		k_eastseaxe = { has_holder = no }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = essex_assigned }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			NOT = { has_global_flag = essex_created }
			NAND = {
				has_landed_title = d_eastseaxe
				has_landed_title = d_middleseaxe
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { has_global_flag = essex_created }
			num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			completely_controls = c_londinium
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			NOT = {
				prestige = 400
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			NOT = {
				culture = oldsaxon
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			NOT = {
				completely_controls = c_londinium
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = essex_assigned
		k_eastseaxe = { gain_title = ROOT }
		wealth = 100
		character_event = { id = 31205 }
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = no
			age = 35
			attributes = {
				martial = 11
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
		}
		location = { 
			new_character = {
				spawn_unit = {
					province = PREV
					troops =
					{
						heavy_infantry = { 500 500 }
						pikemen = { 300 300 }
					}
					attrition = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_landed_title = d_eastseaxe } }
			add_claim = d_eastseaxe
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

# Creation of the Jarldom of Deira
narrative_event = {
	id = 314111
	title = "EVTNAME314111"
	desc = "EVTDESC314111"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_rivers_landscape"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = d_deira
		NOT = { has_global_flag = deira_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = jorvik_created }
			}
			c_eburacum = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_petuaria = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_iserium = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_cataractonium = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_derventio = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_delgovicia = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_dictium = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
		}
		
		d_ebrauc = { destroy_landed_title = d_ebrauc }
		d_deira = { de_jure_liege = k_northumbria }
		
		set_global_flag = deira_created
		
		if = {						# Creation by Bretwalda of Aenglaland
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_aengland
					ai = yes
					any_vassal = { has_landed_title = k_northumbria }
				}
			}
			k_northumbria = {
				holder_scope = {
					d_deira = {
						grant_title = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314111"
	}
}

		set_global_flag = westcantware_created
		
		if = {						# Creation by Bretwalda of Aenglaland
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_aengland
					ai = yes
					any_vassal = { has_landed_title = k_sussex }
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = cantia_created }
			}
			k_sussex = {
				holder_scope = {
					d_westcantware = {
						grant_title = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {

			has_landed_title = d_southumbria

		}
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		NOT = { trait = imbecile }
		NOT = { trait = blinded }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
		NOT = { has_landed_title = k_northumbria }

		NOT = { has_character_flag = northumbria_assigned }
	}

	}

		wealth = 100

			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random

			culture = ROOT
			employer = k_northumbria
			female = no
			age = 35
			attributes = {
				martial = 11
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
		}
		location = { 
			new_character = {

					province = PREV

					{
						heavy_infantry = { 400 400 }
						pikemen = { 300 300 }
					}
					attrition = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}

}

	min_age = 15

		NOT = { realm_size = 40 }
		NOT = { num_of_king_titles = 2 }
		NOT = { is_title_active = d_spears_of_bernicia }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	
	immediate = {
		activate_title = { title = d_spears_of_bernicia status = yes }
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			employer = k_northumbria
			female = no
			age = 35
			attributes = {
				martial = 12
				diplomacy = 12
				stewardship = 10
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = loyal
			trait = rough_terrain_leader
			trait = lustful
		}
		new_character = {
			d_spears_of_bernicia = { 
				gain_title = PREV
			}
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		}
		d_spears_of_bernicia = { 
			holder_scope = {
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3141151"
		k_northumbria = { holder_scope = { prestige = 50 } }
	}
}

	title = "EVTNAME3121618"
	desc = "EVTDESC3121618"
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	only_playable = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		e_aengland = { has_holder = no }
		has_global_flag = HK_aengland_claim
		NOT = { has_character_flag = HK_aengland_claimant }
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
			has_landed_title = k_east_anglia
			has_landed_title = k_cantia
			has_landed_title = k_mercia

			any_playable_ruler = { has_character_flag = HK_aengland_oppositor }
		}
	}

	immediate = {

			ROOT = {
				set_character_flag = HK_aengland_voter
			}
		}
	}

letter_event = {			# Negative Response
	id = 3121638
	desc = "EVTDESC3121638"
	picture = GFX_evt_letter
	
	only_playable = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_character_flag = HK_aengland_claimant
		FROM = { has_character_flag = HK_aengland_oppositor }
	}
	
	option = {					# Accept dispute and stand down
		name = "EVTOPTA3121638"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					is_HK_aengland_relevant_trigger = yes
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
				}
				character_event = { id = 3121688 }
			}
		}
		prestige = -25

		k_rheged = { de_jure_liege = e_hen_ogledd }
		k_pennines = { de_jure_liege = e_hen_ogledd }
		k_ebrauc = { de_jure_liege = e_hen_ogledd }
		k_elmet = { de_jure_liege = e_hen_ogledd }
		k_ynys_man = { de_jure_liege = e_hen_ogledd }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = alba_formed } }
			k_strathclyde = { de_jure_liege = e_hen_ogledd }
			k_lothian = { de_jure_liege = e_hen_ogledd }
		}

		k_siluria = {
			set_name = "Glywysing"
			adjective = "Glywysing"
		}
	}
	
	option = {						# Anglo-Saxons
		name = "EVTOPTA3122101"
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {						# Britons
		name = "EVTOPTB3122101"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {						# Others
		name = "EVTOPTB3122101"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					culture = briton
					culture = romanobritish
					culture = cumbrian
					is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

narrative_event = {	# Creation of Imperium Galliarum
	id = 3152100
	title = "EVTNAME3152100"
	desc = "EVTDESC3152100"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_roman_army_aquila"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = e_gaul
		NOT = { has_global_flag = imperium_galliarum_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = imperium_galliarum_created
		clr_global_flag = romanized_germanic_empire_formed
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored } }
			restore_roman_provinces_gaul_effect = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = k_gaul }
			destroy_landed_title = k_gaul 
		}
		
		any_title = {
			limit = { has_title_flag = gallic_province }
			de_jure_liege = e_gaul
		}
		
		e_gaul = {
			holder_scope = { set_character_flag = created_roman_empire_title }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3152100"
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				has_landed_title = e_gaul
				top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_gaul }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_landed_title = e_gaul
				has_landed_title = k_gaul
			}
			k_gaul = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB3152100"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_landed_title = e_gaul
					top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_gaul }
				}
			}
			culture = roman
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC3152100"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_landed_title = e_gaul
					top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_gaul }
				}
			}
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = roman }
			capital_scope = {
				region = world_ireland
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD3152100"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_landed_title = e_gaul
					top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_gaul }
				}
			}
			NOT = { culture = roman }
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = {
				capital_scope = {
					region = world_ireland
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTE3152100"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_landed_title = e_gaul
					top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_gaul }
				}
			}
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}	
	}
}

narrative_event = {	# Reconquest of Benoic
	id = 314190
	title = "EVTNAME314190"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_coastal"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC314190
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored } }
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC314190_1
		trigger = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored }
	}
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		OR = {
			is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
			has_landed_title = e_visigoths
		}
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = k_benoic
			any_vassal = { has_landed_title = k_benoic }
			AND = {
				k_benoic = { has_holder = no }
				completely_controls_region = custom_benoic
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = benoic_renamed }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = benoic_destroyed }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		k_benoic = {
			destroy_landed_title = k_benoic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored } }
			d_normannia = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
			d_trebes = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
			d_redonia = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }

		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored }
			d_normannia = { de_jure_liege = k_lugdunesis_secunda }
			d_trebes = { de_jure_liege = k_lugdunesis_secunda }
			d_redonia = { de_jure_liege = k_lugdunesis_tertia }
		}
		
		d_trebes = {
			set_name = "Abrincatuia"
			adjective = "Abrincatuian"
		}
		
		set_global_flag = benoic_renamed
		clr_global_flag = benoic_destroyed
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314190"
		trigger = {
			culture_group = imperiale
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314190"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				culture_group = imperiale
				culture = armorican
				culture = breton
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC314191"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = armorican
				culture = breton
			}
		}	
	}
}

				d_redonia = { de_jure_liege = k_lugdunesis_tertia }
			}
		}
		d_broerec = {
			set_name = "Venetia"
			adjective = "Venetian"
		}
		d_domnonea = {
			set_name = "Curiosolitia"
			adjective = "Curiosolitian"

			d_glannativia = { de_jure_liege = k_alpes_maritimae }
			d_vintiensia = { de_jure_liege = k_alpes_maritimae }
			d_antipolitania = { de_jure_liege = k_alpes_maritimae }
			d_cemelenensia = { de_jure_liege = k_alpes_maritimae }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA318100"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = imperiale
					NOT = { top_liege = { has_landed_title = k_praetorian_prefecture_of_gaul } }
				}
				top_liege = { character = ROOT }
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB318100"
		trigger = {
			NOR = { 
				top_liege = { character = ROOT }
				culture_group = imperiale
				AND = {
					culture = burgundian
					has_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_burgundy
				}
				AND = {
					culture = visigoth
					has_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_visigoths
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						culture = ostrogoth
						top_liege = { has_landed_title = k_praetorian_prefecture_of_gaul }
					}
					has_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_ostrogoths
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC318100"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					culture = burgundian
					has_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_burgundy
				}
				AND = {
					culture = visigoth
					has_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_visigoths
				}

					}
					has_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_ostrogoths
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_burgundy
		clr_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_ostrogoths
		clr_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_visigoths
	}

	id = 318105
	title = "EVTNAME318105"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC318105
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored } 
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC318105_1
		trigger = { 
			has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored 
		}
	}
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_roman_aquila_pillar"
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_independent = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = e_gaul
			has_landed_title = e_roman_britannia
			has_landed_title = k_gaul
			has_landed_title = e_visigoths
		}
		has_global_flag = maxima_sequanorum_conquered_burgundy
		NOT = { 
			primary_title = {
				title = k_burgundy
			}
		}
		completely_controls_region = world_gaul_maxima_sequanorum
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored } }
			d_sequania = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
			d_equestria = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
			d_helvitioria = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
			d_rauricia = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored }
			d_sequania = { de_jure_liege = k_maxima_sequanorum }
			d_equestria = { de_jure_liege = k_maxima_sequanorum }
			d_helvitioria = { de_jure_liege = k_maxima_sequanorum }
			d_rauricia = { de_jure_liege = k_maxima_sequanorum }
		}
		clr_global_flag = maxima_sequanorum_conquered_burgundy
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA318100"
		trigger = {
			culture_group = imperiale
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB318100"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				culture_group = imperiale
				culture = burgundian
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC318100"
		trigger = {
			culture = burgundian
		}	
	}

	desc = "EVTDESC314514"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_traveller_hills"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
		completely_controls = c_ratae
		completely_controls = c_causennae
		completely_controls = c_trent_hills
		independent = yes
		NOT = { has_global_flag = middleangles_created }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = lerion_renamed }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		d_lerion = { de_jure_liege = k_flavia_cesariensis }
		d_lerion = {
			set_name = "Corieltauvia"
			adjective = "Corieltauvian"
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOR = { 
					has_global_flag = pegansaete_created 
					has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created
				} 
			}
			c_trent_hills = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOR = { 
					has_global_flag = grentbryce_created 
					has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created
				} 
			}
			c_the_fens = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
			c_holland = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = tomsaete_created } }
			c_repton = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
			c_manduessedum = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = hwicce_created } }
			c_tripontium = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		}
		
		set_global_flag = lerion_renamed
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314514"
		trigger = {
			is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314514"

		}	
	}

# Creation of Hibernia Prima
narrative_event = {	
	id = 314561
	title = "EVTNAME314561"
	desc = "EVTDESC314561"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_roman_legion_marching"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = k_hibernia_prima
		NOT = { has_global_flag = hibernia_prima_restored }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {		
		set_global_flag = hibernia_prima_restored
		k_hibernia_prima = { capital_scope = { province_event = { id = 315191 days = 5500 random = 1800 } }	}	# Convert culture of capital
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314561"
		trigger = {
			has_landed_title = k_hibernia_prima
		}	
		prestige = 100
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314561"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = imperiale
				top_liege = {
					is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes		
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_hibernia_prima }
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC314561"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = imperiale
					top_liege = {
						is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes		
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_hibernia_prima }
		}	
	}
}

# Conquest of Soissons
narrative_event = {
	id = 314201
	title = "EVTNAME314201"
	desc = EVTDESC314201
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_valley_autumn"
	
	only_playable = yes

# Conquest of Benoic
narrative_event = {
	id = 314202
	title = "EVTNAME314202"
	desc = "EVTDESC314202"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_forest_light"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		c_ynys_trebes = { de_jure_liege = d_normanz }
		c_abrincatae = { de_jure_liege = d_normanz }
		c_caesarea = { de_jure_liege = d_normanz }
		c_constantia = { de_jure_liege = d_normanz }
		c_alauna = { de_jure_liege = d_normanz }
		c_rennes = { de_jure_liege = d_rennes }
		c_sipia = { de_jure_liege = d_rennes }
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			k_benoic = {
				any_de_jure_vassal_title = {
					limit = { higher_tier_than = COUNT }
					destroy_landed_title_and_transfer_vassals_to_liege_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		d_normannia = { de_jure_liege = k_broceliande }
		d_trebes = { de_jure_liege = k_broceliande }
		d_redonia = { de_jure_liege = k_broceliande }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = broceliande_renamed 
				NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored }
			}
			d_normannia = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
			d_trebes = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
			d_redonia = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = broceliande_renamed 
				has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored
			}
			d_normannia = { de_jure_liege = k_lugdunesis_secunda }
			d_trebes = { de_jure_liege = k_lugdunesis_secunda }
			d_redonia = { de_jure_liege = k_lugdunesis_tertia }
		}
		
		set_global_flag = benoic_conquered
		set_global_flag = benoic_destroyed
		set_global_flag = normanz_created
		set_global_flag = rennes_created
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314202"
		trigger = {
			is_frankish_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314202"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = armorican
				culture = breton
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC314202"
		trigger = {
			NOR = { 
				is_frankish_culture_trigger = yes
				culture = armorican
				culture = breton
			}
		}
	}
}
	

# Creation of the Duchy of Bretland/Eorldom of Lidwic
narrative_event = {
	id = 314203
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_forest_light"
	
	title = {
		text = EVTNAME314203
		trigger = {
			ROOT = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no } }
		}
	}
	
	title = {
		text = EVTNAME314203_1
		trigger = {
			ROOT = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes } }
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC314203
		trigger = {
			ROOT = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no } }
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC314203_1
		trigger = {
			ROOT = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes } }
		}
	}
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = d_bretagne
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = bretagne_created }
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = saxon_bretagne
				top_liege = { 
					is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no 
					in_revolt = no
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = saxon_bretagne }
				top_liege = { 
					is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
					in_revolt = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c_blavia = { de_jure_liege = d_bretagne }
		c_vannes = { de_jure_liege = d_bretagne }
		c_cornugallia = { de_jure_liege = d_bretagne }
		c_brivates = { de_jure_liege = d_bretagne }
		c_quimper = { de_jure_liege = d_bretagne }
		c_armorica = { de_jure_liege = d_bretagne }
		c_poutrocoet = { de_jure_liege = d_bretagne }
		c_broceliande = { de_jure_liege = d_bretagne }
		c_fanum_martis = { de_jure_liege = d_bretagne }
		if = {
			limit = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no } }
			d_bretagne = { de_jure_liege = k_neustria }
			clr_global_flag = saxon_bretagne
		}
		if = {
			limit = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes } }
			d_bretagne = { de_jure_liege = k_saxon_gaul }
			set_global_flag = saxon_bretagne
		}
		
		d_finis_terrae = { destroy_landed_title = d_finis_terrae }
		d_broerec = { destroy_landed_title = d_broerec }
		d_domnonea = { destroy_landed_title = d_domnonea }
		
		set_global_flag = bretagne_created
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314203"
	}
}

	title = "EVTNAME314206"
	desc = "EVTDESC314206"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_coastal_town"

			d_avignon = { de_jure_liege = k_provence }

			d_embrum = { de_jure_liege = k_provence }

			c_dinia = { de_jure_liege = d_frejus }
			c_sanitium = { de_jure_liege = d_frejus }
			c_glanate = { de_jure_liege = d_antibes }
			c_vintium = { de_jure_liege = d_antibes }

			c_cemenelum = { de_jure_liege = d_antibes }

			d_marseille = { de_jure_liege = k_provence }
			d_frejus = { de_jure_liege = k_provence }
			d_antibes = { de_jure_liege = k_provence }
			
			set_global_flag = arles_created
			set_global_flag = marseille_created
			set_global_flag = frejus_created
			set_global_flag = antibes_created
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			k_praetorian_prefecture_of_gaul = {
				any_de_jure_vassal_title = {
					limit = { higher_tier_than = COUNT }

								limit = { independent = yes	}
								top_liege = {
									set_defacto_vassal = PREVPREV
								}
							}
						}			
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							capital_scope = {
								owner = {
									top_liege = {
										character = ROOT
									}
								}
							}
						}
						destroy_landed_title = THIS
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		set_global_flag = provence_conquered 
	}

		name = "EVTOPTA314206"

# Subjugation of Frisia
narrative_event = {
	id = 314207
	title = "EVTNAME314207"
	desc = "EVTDESC314207"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_lord_overlooking_bridge"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		is_frankish_culture_trigger = yes
		NOT = { top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_germania } }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = frisia_subjugated }
		completely_controls_region = custom_frisia
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = { 
		set_global_flag = frisia_subjugated 
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = saxony_expanded }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = hamaland_conquered_saxon }
					has_global_flag = saxony_subjugated
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = saxony_expanded
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_chamavia } }
				d_hamaland = { de_jure_liege = k_frisia }
			}
			d_salland = { de_jure_liege = k_frisia }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = flanders_created }
			c_aardenburg = { de_jure_liege = d_flandres }
			c_wasia = { de_jure_liege = d_flandres }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = flanders_created } }
			c_wasia = { de_jure_liege = d_toxandria }
			c_aardenburg = { de_jure_liege = d_menapia }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = western_roman_empire_fallen }
			k_frisia = { de_jure_liege = e_franks }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314207"
	}
}

		NOT = { top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_germania } }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = saxony_subjugated }

				d_hamaland = { de_jure_liege = k_frisia }

		}
	}
	
	option = {

	}

	}
	
	immediate = { 
		set_global_flag = alemannia_subjugated
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = franconia_expanded } }
			set_global_flag = franconia_expanded
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = franconia_created } }
				d_wormsgau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
				d_speyergau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = rheingau_renamed } }
					d_rheingau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ufgau_renamed } }
					d_ufgau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = elsenzgau_renamed } }
					d_elsenzgau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
				}
				d_wingarteiba = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = waldsassengau_renamed } }
					d_waldsassengau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = kochergau_renamed } }
					d_kochergau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
				}
			}
			else = {
				d_wormsgau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
				d_speyergau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = rheingau_renamed } }
					d_rheingau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ufgau_renamed } }
					d_ufgau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = elsenzgau_renamed } }
					d_elsenzgau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
				}
				d_wingarteiba = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = waldsassengau_renamed } }
					d_waldsassengau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = kochergau_renamed } }
					d_kochergau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = western_roman_empire_fallen }
			k_alemannia = { de_jure_liege = e_franks }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314210"
	}
}

# Conquest of Franconia
narrative_event = {
	id = 314211
	title = "EVTNAME314211"
	desc = "EVTDESC314211"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_battle_visigoths"
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_independent = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		is_frankish_culture_trigger = yes
		NOT = { top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_germania } }
		has_global_flag = franconia_created
		completely_controls_region = custom_ripuaria
		completely_controls_region = world_hesse
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = franconia_expanded
			AND = {
				completely_controls_region = world_south_franconia
				completely_controls_region = custom_west_franconia
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = { 
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = hesse_renamed } }
			d_hesse = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
		}
		d_lahngau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
		d_wetterau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = franconia_expanded }
			d_wormsgau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
			d_speyergau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = rheingau_renamed } }
				d_rheingau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ufgau_renamed } }
				d_ufgau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = elsenzgau_renamed } }
				d_elsenzgau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
			}
			d_wingarteiba = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = waldsassengau_renamed } }
				d_waldsassengau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = kochergau_renamed } }
				d_kochergau = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_bructeria } }
			d_brukterer = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
		}
		d_cologne = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = soissons_conquered } }
			d_bracbant = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
		}
		else = {
			d_bracbant = { de_jure_liege = k_franks }
		}
		clr_global_flag = franconia_created
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314211"
	}
}

				d_redonia = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }

				d_trebes = { de_jure_liege = k_lugdunesis_secunda }

# Creation of the County of Picard/Eorldom of Ambeanas
narrative_event = {
	id = 314221
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_valley_autumn"
	
	title = {
		text = EVTNAME314221
		trigger = {
			ROOT = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no } }
		}
	}
	
	title = {
		text = EVTNAME314221_1
		trigger = {
			ROOT = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes } }
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC314221
		trigger = {
			ROOT = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no } }
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC314221_1
		trigger = {
			ROOT = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes } }
		}
	}
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = d_picard
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = picard_created }
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = saxon_picard
				top_liege = { 
					is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
					in_revolt = no
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = saxon_picard }
				top_liege = { 
					is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
					in_revolt = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c_samarobriva = { de_jure_liege = d_picard }
		c_litomagus = { de_jure_liege = d_picard }
		c_pontes_ambianorum = { de_jure_liege = d_picard }
		c_leuconaus = { de_jure_liege = d_picard }
		if = {
			limit = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no } }
			d_picard = { de_jure_liege = k_neustria }
			clr_global_flag = saxon_picard
		}
		if = {
			limit = { top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes } }
			d_picard = { de_jure_liege = k_saxon_gaul }
			set_global_flag = saxon_picard
		}
		
		d_ambiania = { 
			destroy_landed_title = THIS			
		}
		
		set_global_flag = picard_created
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314221"
	}
}

		c_ghent = { de_jure_liege = d_flandres }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = frisia_subjugated }
			c_aardenburg = { de_jure_liege = d_flandres }
			c_wasia = { de_jure_liege = d_flandres }
		}
		d_flandres = { de_jure_liege = k_franks }
		
		set_global_flag = flanders_created

narrative_event = {	# Conquest of Aquitania Prima
	id = 314700
	title = "EVTNAME314700"
	desc = EVTDESC314700
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_battle_visigoths"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = k_visigoths
		top_liege = { 
			NOR = {
				is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
				has_landed_title = e_visigoths
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = aquitaniaprima_conquered_visigoths }
		completely_controls_region = world_gaul_aquitania_prima
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = aquitaniaprima_conquered_visigoths
		d_biturigia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_lemovicia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_alvernia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_gabalia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_vellavia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_cadurcia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_rutenia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_albigensia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314700"
		trigger = {
			culture = visigoth
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314700"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				culture_group = imperiale
				culture = visigoth
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC314700"
		trigger = {
			culture_group = imperiale
		}	
	}
}

narrative_event = {	# Conquest of Aquitania Tertia
	id = 314704
	title = "EVTNAME314704"
	desc = EVTDESC314704
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_hill"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = k_visigoths
		top_liege = { 
			NOR = {
				is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
				has_landed_title = e_visigoths
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = aquitania_tertia_conquered_visigoths }
		NAND = {
			has_landed_title = k_basque_vasconia
			has_global_flag = basque_vasconia_created
		}
		completely_controls_region = world_gaul_aquitania_tertia
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = aquitania_tertia_conquered_visigoths
		d_elusatia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_auscia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_lactoratia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_convenia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_consorannia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_bigerria = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_aturensia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_vasatia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_benearia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_iluronensia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_boiatia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		d_tarbellia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = aquitania_created 
				has_global_flag = basque_vasconia_created
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_global_flag = aquitania_secunda_conquered_visigoths }
					NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored }
				}
				d_viviscia = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
				d_nitiobrogia = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_global_flag = aquitania_secunda_conquered_visigoths }
					has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored
				}
				d_viviscia = { de_jure_liege = k_aquitania_secunda }
				d_nitiobrogia = { de_jure_liege = k_aquitania_secunda }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = aquitania_secunda_conquered_visigoths }
				d_viviscia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
				d_nitiobrogia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = basque_vasconia_created
		destroy_landed_title = k_basque_vasconia
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314704"
		trigger = {
			culture = visigoth
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314704"
		trigger = {
			NOR = { 
				culture_group = imperiale
				culture_group = basque
				culture = visigoth
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC314704"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = imperiale
				culture_group = basque
			}
		}	
	}
}

narrative_event = {	# Romanized Germanic claims the Empire
	id = 314749
	title = "EVTNAME314749"
	desc = EVTDESC314749
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_roman_emperor_salute"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = romanized_germanic_empire_formed
		clr_global_flag = imperium_galliarum_created
		
		# Set de jure structure
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = k_visigoths }
			clr_global_flag = aquitaniaprima_conquered_visigoths
			clr_global_flag = tolosa_conquered_visigoths
			clr_global_flag = aquitania_secunda_conquered_visigoths
			clr_global_flag = aquitania_tertia_conquered_visigoths
			clr_global_flag = septimania_conquered_visigoths
			clr_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_visigoths
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = k_burgundy }
			clr_global_flag = lugdunensisprima_conquered_burgundy
			clr_global_flag = maxima_sequanorum_conquered_burgundy
			clr_global_flag = viennensisprima_conquered_burgundy
			clr_global_flag = northern_provence_conquered_burgundy
			clr_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_burgundy
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = k_ostrogoths }
			clr_global_flag = northern_provence_conquered_ostrogoths
			clr_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_ostrogoths
		}
		#if = {
			#limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored } }
			restore_roman_provinces_gaul_effect = yes
		#}
		any_title = {
			limit = { has_title_flag = gallic_province }
			de_jure_liege = e_visigoths
		}
		
		# Rename title and remove previous empire claiming if appropriate
		activate_title = { title = e_visigoths status = yes }
		primary_title = {
			capital_scope = { e_visigoths = { set_preferred_capital = PREV } }
			e_visigoths = { 
				set_coa = PREV 
				clear_flags_with_prefix = empire_claimed_
			}
			if = {
				limit = { title = k_visigoths }
				e_visigoths = {
					set_name = ""
					adjective = ""
					set_title_flag = empire_claimed_visigoths
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { title = k_ostrogoths }
				e_visigoths = {
					set_name = "Ostrogothic Empire"
					adjective = "Ostrogothic"
					set_title_flag = empire_claimed_ostrogoths
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { title = k_burgundy }
				e_visigoths = {
					set_name = "Burgundian Empire"
					adjective = "Burgundian"
					set_title_flag = empire_claimed_burgundians
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { title = k_taifals }
				e_visigoths = {
					set_name = "Taifal Empire"
					adjective = "Taifal"
					set_title_flag = empire_claimed_taifals
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { title = k_alans }
				e_visigoths = {
					set_name = "Alan Empire"
					adjective = "Alan"
					set_title_flag = empire_claimed_alans
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_title = {
			limit = { has_title_flag = romanized_germanic_empire_created_from_title } 
			clr_title_flag = romanized_germanic_empire_created_from_title
		}
		primary_title = { set_title_flag = romanized_germanic_empire_created_from_title }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314749"
		trigger = {
			character = ROOT
		}	
		prestige = 500
		e_visigoths = { gain_title = ROOT }
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					title = k_visigoths
					title = k_ostrogoths
					title = k_burgundy
					title = k_taifals
					title = k_alans
				}
			}
			destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314749"
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				character = ROOT
			}
			NOT = { character = ROOT }
			NOT = { culture_group = imperiale }
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314749"
		trigger = {
			culture_group = imperiale
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC314749"
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				culture_group = imperiale
				top_liege = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}	
	}
}

	title = "EVTNAME318300"
	desc = EVTDESC318300

	only_playable = yes

		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = k_burgundy

			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = lugdunensisprima_conquered_burgundy }

			d_ebrodunensia = { de_jure_liege = k_burgundy }
		}
		else = {
			set_global_flag = northern_provence_conquered_ostrogoths
			d_avenionensia = { de_jure_liege = k_praetorian_prefecture_of_gaul }
			d_arausicensia = { de_jure_liege = k_praetorian_prefecture_of_gaul }

			d_antipolitania = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }
			d_cemelenensia = { de_jure_liege = k_visigoths }

			set_global_flag = southern_provence_conquered_burgundy
			d_arelatensia = { de_jure_liege = k_burgundy }
			d_massiliensia = { de_jure_liege = k_burgundy }

			d_diniensia = { de_jure_liege = k_praetorian_prefecture_of_gaul }
			d_sanitiensia = { de_jure_liege = k_praetorian_prefecture_of_gaul }
			d_glannativia = { de_jure_liege = k_praetorian_prefecture_of_gaul }

### GERMANIA ###

# Creation of the Empire of Germania
narrative_event = {
	id = 314825
	title = "EVTNAME314825"
	desc = "EVTDESC314825"
	picture = "GFX_evt_germansite"
	
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = e_germania
		NOT = { has_global_flag = germania_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = germania_created
		
		k_frisia = { de_jure_liege = e_germania }
		clr_global_flag = frisia_subjugated
		
		k_saxony = { de_jure_liege = e_germania }
		clr_global_flag = saxony_subjugated
		
		activate_title = { title = k_franconia status = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = hesse_renamed } }
			d_hesse = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		}
		d_lahngau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		d_wetterau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = franconia_expanded }
			d_wormsgau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			d_speyergau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = rheingau_renamed } }
				d_rheingau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ufgau_renamed } }
				d_ufgau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = elsenzgau_renamed } }
				d_elsenzgau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
			d_wingarteiba = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = waldsassengau_renamed } }
				d_waldsassengau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = kochergau_renamed } }
				d_kochergau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_bructeria } }
			d_brukterer = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		}
		d_cologne = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		d_bracbant = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		set_global_flag = franconia_created
		
		k_alemannia = { de_jure_liege = e_germania }
		clr_global_flag = alemannia_subjugated
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314825"
		trigger = { has_landed_title = e_germania }
		prestige = 200
	}	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314825"
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_landed_title = e_germania }
			top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_germania }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC314825"
		trigger = {
			culture_group = germanic
			NOT = { top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_germania } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD314825"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
				culture_group = imperiale
			}
			NOT = { top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_germania } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTE314825"
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				culture_group = germanic
				is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
				culture_group = imperiale
				top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_germania }
			}
		}
	}

# Reconquest of Franconia
narrative_event = {
	id = 314829
	title = "EVTNAME314829"
	desc = "EVTDESC314829"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_battle_visigoths"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = e_germania
		has_global_flag = germania_created
		NOT = { has_landed_title = e_franks }
		completely_controls_region = world_hesse
		completely_controls_region = custom_ripuaria
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = franconia_expanded
			AND = {
				completely_controls_region = world_south_franconia
				completely_controls_region = custom_west_franconia
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = franconia_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = franconia_created
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = hesse_renamed } }
			d_hesse = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		}
		d_lahngau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		d_wetterau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = franconia_expanded }
			d_wormsgau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			d_speyergau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = rheingau_renamed } }
				d_rheingau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ufgau_renamed } }
				d_ufgau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = elsenzgau_renamed } }
				d_elsenzgau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
			d_wingarteiba = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = waldsassengau_renamed } }
				d_waldsassengau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = kochergau_renamed } }
				d_kochergau = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_bructeria } }
			d_brukterer = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		}
		d_cologne = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
		d_bracbant = { de_jure_liege = k_franconia }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314829"
	}
}

	}
	
	immediate = {
		d_elusatia = { de_jure_liege = k_basque_vasconia }

		d_boiatia = { de_jure_liege = k_basque_vasconia }
		d_tarbellia = { de_jure_liege = k_basque_vasconia }

			d_nitiobrogia = { de_jure_liege = k_basque_vasconia }

			}
		}
	}

# Creation of the High Kingdom of Scandinavia
narrative_event = {
	id = 314804
	title = "EVTNAME314804"
	desc = "EVTDESC314804"
	picture = "GFX_evt_viking_throneroom_oldgods"
	
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = scandinavia_created
		e_denmark = {
			any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = {
				limit = { tier = KING }
				de_jure_liege = e_scandinavia
			}
		}
		e_norway = {
			any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = {
				limit = { tier = KING }
				de_jure_liege = e_scandinavia
			}
		}
		e_sweden = {
			any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = {
				limit = { tier = KING }
				de_jure_liege = e_scandinavia
			}
		}
		e_geatland = {
			any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = {
				limit = { tier = KING }
				de_jure_liege = e_scandinavia
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314804"
		trigger = { has_landed_title = e_scandinavia }
		prestige = 300
		e_denmark = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
		e_norway = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
		e_sweden = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
		e_geatland = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314804"
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_landed_title = e_scandinavia }
			top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_scandinavia }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC314804"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_scandinavia }
			}
			is_north_germanic_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD314804"
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_scandinavia }
				is_north_germanic_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Rename Broceliande to Breizh under a Breton
narrative_event = {
	id = 314430
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."	
	picture = "GFX_evt_rivers_landscape"
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		culture = breton
		has_landed_title = k_broceliande
		NOT = { has_global_flag = broceliande_renamed_breton }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_alternate_start = no }		# VERY IMPORTANT: PUTTING THIS IN THE TRIGGER INSTEAD CAUSES A CRASH!
			k_broceliande = {
				set_name = "Breizh"
				adjective = "Breton"
			}
		}
		
		set_global_flag = broceliande_renamed_breton
	}
}

	id = 314440
	title = "EVTNAME314440"
	desc = "EVTDESC314440"
	picture = GFX_evt_armorica
	
	only_playable = yes
	major = yes
	only_men = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = armorica_created }
		has_landed_title = e_armorica
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		k_benoic = { de_jure_liege = e_armorica }
		k_broceliande = { de_jure_liege = e_armorica }
		set_global_flag = armorica_created
		clr_global_flag = armorica_conquered_britannia
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314440"		# High King
		trigger = {
			has_landed_title = e_armorica
		}
		prestige = 200
	}
		
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB314440"		# Vassals of the High King
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_landed_title = e_armorica }
			OR = {
				liege = { has_landed_title = e_armorica }
				top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_armorica }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC314440"		# Other Rulers
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_landed_title = e_armorica
				liege = { has_landed_title = e_armorica }
				top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_armorica }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC314462"
	major = yes

			d_osmaeliog = {
				any_de_jure_vassal_title = {

							has_landed_title = k_henis_wyren

								has_landed_title = k_henis_wyren
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		completely_controls = d_osmaeliog
	}

		k_henis_wyren = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
		clr_global_flag = henis_wyren_created
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA314462"
	}

### Brotherhood of Britain ###
narrative_event = {		# Form the Brotherhood (triggered by decision)
	id = 3121659
	title = "EVTNAME3121659"
	desc = "EVTDESC3121659"
	picture = "GFX_evt_warband_on_hill"
	
	major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_landed_title = e_britannia
		NOT = { is_title_active = d_warriors_of_britain }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		activate_title = { title = d_warriors_of_britain status = yes }
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			dynasty = random
			employer = e_britannia
			religion = ROOT
			culture = romanobritish
			female = no
			age = 36
			attributes = {
				martial = 11
				diplomacy = 10
				stewardship = 11
				intrigue = 11
				learning = 12
			}
			trait = skilled_tactician
			trait = skilled_warrior
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = loyal
			trait = inspiring_leader
			# trait = honorable
			trait = honest
		}
		new_character = {
			d_warriors_of_britain = {
				gain_title = PREV
				gender_succ = agnatic
				succession_w_cooldown = open_elective
			}
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3121659"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				character = ROOT
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				top_liege = { character = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB3121659"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					character = ROOT
					culture = briton
					culture = romanobritish
					top_liege = { character = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# High Kingdom of Cymru
narrative_event = {

	only_playable = yes
	major = yes
	min_age = 15
	only_men = yes

		has_landed_title = e_cymru
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = cymru_formed
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB3129168"		# High King
		trigger = {
			has_landed_title = e_cymru
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3129168"		# Vassals of the High King
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_landed_title = e_cymru }
			OR = {
				liege = { has_landed_title = e_cymru }
				top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_cymru }
			}
		}

# High Kingdom of Alba
narrative_event = {		
	id = 3129166
	title = "EVTNAME3129166"
	desc = "EVTDESC3129166"
	picture = GFX_evt_warriors_hills_mist
	
	only_playable = yes
	major = yes
	min_age = 15
	only_men = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = alba_formed }
		has_landed_title = e_alba
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = alba_formed
		clr_global_flag = alba_conquered_britannia
		k_dalriada = { de_jure_liege = e_alba }
		k_caledonia = { de_jure_liege = e_alba }
		k_strathclyde = { de_jure_liege = e_alba }
		k_lothian = { de_jure_liege = e_alba }
		
		# If Dalriada has not been created, integrate the area into Pictavia
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = dalriada_created } }	
			d_hebrides = { de_jure_liege = k_caledonia }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = argyll_renamed } }
				d_argyll = { de_jure_liege = k_caledonia }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB3129166"		# High King
		trigger = {
			has_landed_title = e_alba
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3129166"		# Vassals of the High King
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_landed_title = e_alba }
			OR = {
				liege = { has_landed_title = e_alba }
				top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_alba }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC3129166"		# Other Rulers
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_landed_title = e_alba
					liege = { has_landed_title = e_alba }
					top_liege = { has_landed_title = e_alba }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### RE-CHECKS ###

narrative_event = {	# Lindsey, Pegansaete, Tomsaete, Middle Anglia, Grentbryce
	id = 314270
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	major = no
	hide_new = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	only_playable = no
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 30
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = lindsey_created
			has_global_flag = pegansaete_created
			has_global_flag = tomsaete_created
			has_global_flag = middleangles_created
			has_global_flag = grentbryce_created
		}
		is_alternate_start = no
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = lindsey_created
				NOT = { has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created }
			}
			c_lindum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
			c_caistor = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
			c_ad_abum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
			c_banovallum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
			c_luda = { de_jure_liege = d_lindsey }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = pegansaete_created }
			c_dovedale = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created } }
				c_trent_hills = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
				c_aquae_arnemetiae = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
				c_segelocum = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
				c_scarsdale = { de_jure_liege = d_mercia }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = tomsaete_created }
			c_arden_forest = { de_jure_liege = d_tomsaete }
			c_letocetum = { de_jure_liege = d_tomsaete }
			c_uxacona = { de_jure_liege = d_tomsaete }
			c_manduessedum = { de_jure_liege = d_tomsaete }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created } }
				c_repton = { de_jure_liege = d_tomsaete }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = middleangles_created }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created } }
				c_ratae = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
				c_ad_pontem = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
				c_margidunum = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
				c_vernemetum = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
				c_causennae = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = southernboroughs_created } }
				c_bannaventa = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
				c_gwash = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
				c_ciniubantum = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
			}
			c_brinavae = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
			c_lactodorum = { de_jure_liege = d_middle_angles }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = grentbryce_created
				NOT = { has_global_flag = southernboroughs_created }
			}
			c_godmundceaster = { de_jure_liege = d_grentbryce }
			c_holme_fen = { de_jure_liege = d_grentbryce }
			c_grantabrycge = { de_jure_liege = d_grentbryce }
			c_durobrivae = { de_jure_liege = d_grentbryce }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = grentbryce_created
				NOT = { has_global_flag = fiveboroughs_created }
			}
